Other Events.</span></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">On September 19, 2025, Walmart Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) was informed that Daniel Danker, Executive Vice President, AI Acceleration, Product and Design, entered into a stock trading plan designed to comply with Rule 10b5-1 under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Plan&#8221;). Rule 10b5-1 trading plans permit individuals who are not in possession of material non-public information to adopt a written pre-arranged plan for transactions in securities under specified conditions and for specified periods of time. Mr. Danker&#8217;s Plan is part of an individual long-term asset diversification, tax, and financial planning strategy, and is in accordance with the Company&#8217;s Insider Trading Policy. Under the terms of the Plan, Mr. Danker will have no discretion or control over the timing or effectuation of any transactions in Company securities pursuant to the Plan.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Under the terms of the Plan, Mr. Danker will sell the number of net shares remaining after taxes are withheld from a vesting of 6,873 restricted shares of the Company&#8217;s common stock on January 13, 2026, and the number of net shares remaining after taxes are withheld from a vesting of 103,103 restricted shares of the Company&#8217;s common stock on August 25, 2026, in both cases selling shares at prevailing market prices. Accordingly, the maximum number of shares to be sold under the Plan is 109,976, less shares withheld for taxes upon vesting.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-align:justify;text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Mr. Danker became subject to the Company&#8217;s stock ownership guidelines upon joining the Company.</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:12pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">  </span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">The transactions contemplated by the Plan are in accordance with the Guidelines, under which Mr. Danker is required to own Company stock equal in value to at least five times his base salary by the fifth anniversary of his hire date.</span></div><div><span><br/></span></div><div style="text-indent:36pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Times New Roman',serif;font-size:10pt;font-weight:400;line-height:112%">Any transactions under the Plan will be disclosed publicly
